Introduction\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-1-introduction\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: 1. Introduction\" href=\"#1-introduction\"\u003e\u003csvg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eSwagger™  is a project used to describe and document RESTful APIs.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe Swagger specification defines a set of files required to describe such an API. These files can then be used by the Swagger-UI project to display the API and Swagger-Codegen to generate clients in various languages. Additional utilities can also take advantage of the resulting files, such as testing tools.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e2. Definitions\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-3-definitions\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: 3. The entity can represent an actual object (pets, users..) or a set of logical operations collated together. It is up to the specification user to decide whether sub-resources should be referred to as part of their main resource or as a resource of their own.\nFor example, assume the following URL set:\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-text-roff notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"- /users      - GET\n              POST\n- /users/{id} - GET\n              PATCH\n              DELETE\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e- /users      - GET\n              POST\n- /users/{id} - GET\n              PATCH\n              DELETE\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIn this case, there's either one \"/users\" resource that contains operations on the \"/users/{id}\" sub-resource, or two separate resources.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eURL: A fully qualified URL.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e4. 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe files describing the RESTful API in accordance with the Swagger specification are represented as JSON objects and conform to the JSON standards.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eFor example, if a field is said to have an array value, the JSON array representation will be used:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"{\n   \u0026quot;field\u0026quot; : [...]\n}\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e{\u003c/span\u003e\n   \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"field\"\u003c/span\u003e : \u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e[\u003c/span\u003e...\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e]\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e}\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003ePlease note that while the API is described using JSON, the input and/or output can be in XML, YAML, plain text, or whichever format you chose to use with your API.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eUnless noted otherwise, all field names in the specification are \u003cstrong\u003ecase sensitive\u003c/strong\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e4.2 File Structure\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-42-file-structure\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: 4.2 File Structure\" href=\"#42-file-structure\"\u003e\u003csvg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe Swagger representation of the API is comprised of two file types:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ca href=\"#51-resource-listing\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eThe Resource Listing\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/a\u003e - This is the root document that contains general API information and lists the resources. Each resource has its own URL that defines the API operations on it.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ca href=\"#52-api-declaration\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eThe API Declaration\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/a\u003e - This document describes a resource, including its API calls and models. There is one file per resource.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e4.3 Data Types\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-43-data-types\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: 4.3 Data Types\" href=\"#43-data-types\"\u003e\u003csvg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIn the Swagger specification, the data types are used in several locations - \u003ca href=\"#523-operation-object\"\u003eOperations\u003c/a\u003e, \u003ca href=\"#524-parameter-object\"\u003eOperation Parameters\u003c/a\u003e, \u003ca href=\"#527-model-object\"\u003eModels\u003c/a\u003e, and within the data types themselves (arrays).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe fields used to describe a given data type are added flatly to the relevant object. For example, if an object Foo has the field \u003ccode\u003ename\u003c/code\u003e, and is also a data type, then it MUST also include the field \u003ccode\u003etype\u003c/code\u003e (or its variance, as explained ahead). In this example, Foo would look like:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"\u0026quot;Foo\u0026quot; : {\n   \u0026quot;name\u0026quot; : \u0026quot;sample\u0026quot;,\n   \u0026quot;type\u0026quot; : \u0026quot;string\u0026quot;,\n   ...\n}\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"Foo\"\u003c/span\u003e : \u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e{\u003c/span\u003e\n   \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"name\"\u003c/span\u003e : \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"sample\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e,\u003c/span\u003e\n   \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"type\"\u003c/span\u003e : \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"string\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e,\u003c/span\u003e\n   ...\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e}\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThis section describes the general fields that are available to describe such data types. Some data types allow additional fields to extend further limitations on the data type \u003cem\u003evalue\u003c/em\u003e (see \u003ca href=\"#433-data-type-fields\"\u003e4.3.3 Data Type Fields\u003c/a\u003e for further details).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eSpecial care should be taken when referencing a model (or a complex type). There are currently two variations, and the proper variation should be documented everywhere the model may be used. This behavior will be unified in future versions of the spec.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe Swagger specification supports five data types:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ca href=\"#431-primitives\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eprimitive\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e (input/output)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003econtainers (as arrays/sets) (input/output)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ca href=\"#527-model-object\"\u003ecomplex\u003c/a\u003e (as \u003ccode\u003emodels\u003c/code\u003e) (input/output)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ca href=\"#432-void\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003evoid\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e (output)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ca href=\"#434-file\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eFile\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e (input)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch4 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e4.3.1 Primitives\u003c/h4\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-431-primitives\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: 4.3.1 Primitives\" href=\"#431-primitives\"\u003e\u003csvg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eDifferent programming languages represent primitives differently. The Swagger specification supports by name only the primitive types supported by the \u003ca href=\"http://json-schema.org/latest/json-schema-core.html#anchor8\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eJSON-Schema Draft 4\u003c/a\u003e. However, in order to allow fine tuning a primitive definition, an additional \u003ca href=\"#dataTypeFormat\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eformat\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e field MAY accompany the \u003ca href=\"#dataTypeType\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003etype\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e primitive to give more information about the type used. If the \u003ca href=\"#dataTypeFormat\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eformat\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e field is used, the respective client MUST conform to the elaborate type.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cmarkdown-accessiblity-table\u003e\u003ctable\u003e\n\u003cthead\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003cth\u003eCommon Name\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003cth\u003e\u003ca class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch4 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e4.3.2 \u003ccode\u003evoid\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/h4\u003e\u003ca As such it MAY be used only for the return type of operations.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch4 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e4.3.3 Data Type Fields\u003c/h4\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-433-data-type-fields\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: 4.3.3 Data Type Fields\" href=\"#433-data-type-fields\"\u003e\u003csvg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAs explained above, when an object is said to include a data type, there are a set of fields it may include (some are required and some are optional).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eSpecial care should be taken when referencing a model (or a complex type). There currently two variations, and the proper variation should be documented everywhere it may be used. This behavior will be unified in future versions of the spec.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe table below shows the available fields to describe a data type. The \u003ccode\u003eValidity\u003c/code\u003e column may impose additional restrictions as to which data type is required in order to include this field. For example, \u003ca href=\"#dataTypeEnum\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eenum\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e may only be included if the \u003ca href=\"#dataTypeType\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003etype\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e field is set to \u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cmarkdown-accessiblity-table\u003e\u003ctable\u003e\n\u003cthead\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003cth\u003eField Name\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003cth align=\"center\"\u003eType\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003cth\u003eValidity\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003cth\u003eDescription\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003c/thead\u003e\n\u003ctbody\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-datatypetype\"\u003etype\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eAny\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eRequired (if \u003ca href=\"#dataTypeRef\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003e$ref\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e is not used).\u003c/strong\u003e The return type of the operation. The value MUST be one of the \u003ca href=\"#431-primitives\"\u003ePrimitives\u003c/a\u003e, \u003ccode\u003earray\u003c/code\u003e or a model's \u003ca href=\"#modelId\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eid\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-datatyperef\"\u003e$ref\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eAny\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eRequired (if \u003ca href=\"#dataTypeType\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003etype\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e is not used).\u003c/strong\u003e The \u003ca href=\"#527-model-object\"\u003eModel\u003c/a\u003e to be used. The value MUST be a model's \u003ca href=\"#modelId\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eid\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-datatypeformat\"\u003eformat\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eprimitive\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eFine-tuned primitive type definition. See \u003ca href=\"#431-primitives\"\u003ePrimitives\u003c/a\u003e for further information. The value MUST be one that is defined under \u003ca href=\"#431-primitives\"\u003ePrimitives\u003c/a\u003e, corresponding to the right primitive \u003ca href=\"#dataTypeType\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003etype\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-datatypedefaultvalue\"\u003edefaultValue\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e\u003cem\u003especial\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eprimitive\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eThe default value to be used for the field. The value type MUST conform with the primitive's \u003ca href=\"#dataTypeType\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003etype\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e value.\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-datatypeenum\"\u003eenum\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e[\u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e]\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eA fixed list of possible values. If this field is used in conjunction with the \u003ca href=\"#dataTypeDefaultValue\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003edefaultValue\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e field, then the default value MUST be one of the values defined in the \u003ccode\u003eenum\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-datatypeminimum\"\u003eminimum\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ccode\u003enumber\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003einteger\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eThe minimum valid value for the type, inclusive. If this field is used in conjunction with the \u003ca href=\"#dataTypeDefaultValue\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003edefaultValue\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e field, then the default value MUST be higher than or equal to this value. The value type is \u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e and should represent the minimum numeric value. \u003cstrong\u003eNote\u003c/strong\u003e: This will change to a numeric value in the future.\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-datatypemaximum\"\u003emaximum\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ccode\u003enumber\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003einteger\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eThe maximum valid value for the type, inclusive. If this field is used in conjunction with the \u003ca href=\"#dataTypeDefaultValue\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003edefaultValue\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e field, then the default value MUST be lower than or equal to this value. The value type is \u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e and should represent the maximum numeric value. \u003cstrong\u003eNote\u003c/strong\u003e: This will change to a numeric value in the future.\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-datatypeitems\"\u003eitems\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e\u003ca href=\"#434-items-object\"\u003eItems Object\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ccode\u003earray\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eRequired.\u003c/strong\u003e The type definition of the values in the container. A container MUST NOT be nested in another container.\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-datatypeuniqueitems\"\u003euniqueItems\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eboolean\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ccode\u003earray\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eA flag to note whether the container allows duplicate values or not. If the value is set to \u003ccode\u003etrue\u003c/code\u003e, then the \u003ccode\u003earray\u003c/code\u003e acts as a set.\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003c/tbody\u003e\n\u003c/table\u003e\u003c/markdown-accessiblity-table\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch4 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e4.3.4 Items Object\u003c/h4\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-434-items-object\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: 4.3.4 Items Object\" href=\"#434-items-object\"\u003e\u003csvg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThis object is used to describe the value types used inside an array. Of the \u003ca href=\"#433-data-type-fields\"\u003eData Type Fields\u003c/a\u003e, it can include either the \u003ca href=\"#dataTypeType\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003etype\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e and \u003ca href=\"#dataTypeFormat\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eformat\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e fields \u003cem\u003eOR\u003c/em\u003e the \u003ca href=\"#dataTypeRef\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003e$ref\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e field (when referencing a model). The rest of the listed Data Type fields are not applicable.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIf the \u003ca href=\"#dataTypeType\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003etype\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e field is included it MUST NOT have the value \u003ccode\u003earray\u003c/code\u003e. There's currently no support for containers within containers.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch5 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" It contains general information about the API and an inventory of the available resources.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eBy default, this document SHOULD be served at the \u003ccode\u003e/api-docs\u003c/code\u003e path.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cmarkdown-accessiblity-table\u003e\u003ctable\u003e\n\u003cthead\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003cth\u003eField Name\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003cth align=\"center\"\u003eType\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003cth\u003eDescription\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003c/thead\u003e\n\u003ctbody\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-rlswaggerversion\"\u003eswaggerVersion\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eRequired.\u003c/strong\u003e Specifies the Swagger Specification version being used. It can be used by the Swagger UI and other clients to interpret the API listing. The value MUST be an existing Swagger specification version. \u003cbr\u003eCurrently, \u003ccode\u003e\"1.0\"\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e\"1.1\"\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e\"1.2\"\u003c/code\u003e are valid values. API.\nCurrently, Swagger supports three authorization schemes - basic authentication, API key and OAuth2.\nThe Authorizations Object is used only to \u003cem\u003edeclare\u003c/em\u003e the available authorization schemes but not say which are required where.\nThe actual authorization restrictions are done at the \u003ca href=\"#52-api-declaration\"\u003eAPI declaration\u003c/a\u003e level.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003ePlease note that the Authorizations Object is an object containing other object definitions and as such is structured as follows:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"{\n   \u0026quot;Authorization1\u0026quot; : {...},\n   \u0026quot;Authorization2\u0026quot; : {...},\n   ...,\n   \u0026quot;AuthorizationN\u0026quot; : {...}\n}\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e}\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e,\u003c/span\u003e\n   \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"Authorization2\"\u003c/span\u003e : \u003cspan The name given to the {Authorization Name} is a friendly name that should be used when referring to the authorization scheme. Currently, the authorization schemes supported are basic authentication, API key and OAuth2.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eWithin OAuth2, the Authorization Code Grant and Implicit Grant are supported.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIn the table below, the \u003ccode\u003eValidity\u003c/code\u003e column imposes additional limitations to the requirement of the \u003ca href=\"#authorizationType\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003etype\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e in order to be able to use that field.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cmarkdown-accessiblity-table\u003e\u003ctable\u003e\n\u003cthead\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003cth\u003eField Name\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003cth align=\"center\"\u003eType\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003cth\u003eValidity\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003cth\u003eDescription\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003c/thead\u003e\n\u003ctbody\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-authorizationtype\"\u003etype\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eAny\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eRequired.\u003c/strong\u003e The type of the authorization scheme. Values MUST be either \u003ccode\u003e\"basicAuth\"\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e\"apiKey\"\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003e\"oauth2\"\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-authorizationpassas\"\u003epassAs\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ccode\u003eapiKey\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eRequired.\u003c/strong\u003e Denotes how the API key must be passed. 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe API Declaration provides information about an API exposed on a resource. There should be one file per \u003ca href=\"#512-resource-object\"\u003eResource\u003c/a\u003e described. The file MUST be served in the URL described by the \u003ca href=\"#aePath\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003epath\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e field.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cmarkdown-accessiblity-table\u003e\u003ctable\u003e\n\u003cthead\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003cth\u003eField Name\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003cth align=\"center\"\u003eType\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003cth\u003eDescription\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003c/thead\u003e\n\u003ctbody\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-adswaggerversion\"\u003eswaggerVersion\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eRequired.\u003c/strong\u003e Specifies the Swagger Specification version being used. It can be used by the Swagger UI and other clients to interpret the API listing. The value MUST be an existing Swagger specification version. \u003cbr\u003eCurrently, \u003ccode\u003e\"1.0\"\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e\"1.1\"\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e\"1.2\"\u003c/code\u003e are valid values.\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-adapiversion\"\u003eapiVersion\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eProvides the version of the application API (not to be confused by the \u003ca href=\"#adSwaggerVersion\"\u003especification version\u003c/a\u003e).\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-adbasepath\"\u003ebasePath\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eRequired.\u003c/strong\u003e The root URL serving the API. This field is important because while it is common to have the Resource Listing and API Declarations on the server providing the APIs themselves, it is not a requirement. The API specifications can be served using static files and not generated by the API server itself, so the URL for serving the API cannot always be derived from the URL serving the API specification. The value SHOULD be in the format of a URL.\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-adresourcepath\"\u003eresourcePath\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eThe \u003cem\u003erelative\u003c/em\u003e path to the resource, from the \u003ca href=\"#adBasePath\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003ebasePath\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e, which this API Specification describes. 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe Operation Object describes a single operation on a \u003ca href=\"#apiPath\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003epath\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIn the \u003ca href=\"#apiOperations\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eoperations\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e array, there MUST be only one \u003ca href=\"#523-operation-object\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eOperation Object\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e per \u003ca href=\"#operationMethod\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003emethod\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThis object includes the \u003ca href=\"#433-data-type-fields\"\u003eData Type Fields\u003c/a\u003e in order to describe the return value of the operation. The \u003ca href=\"#dataTypeType\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003etype\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e field MUST be used to link to other models.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThis is the only object where the \u003ca href=\"#dataTypeType\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003etype\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e MAY have the value of \u003ca href=\"#432-void\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003evoid\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e to indicate that the operation returns no value.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cmarkdown-accessiblity-table\u003e\u003ctable\u003e\n\u003cthead\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003cth\u003eField Name\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003cth align=\"center\"\u003eType\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003cth\u003eDescription\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003c/thead\u003e\n\u003ctbody\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-operationmethod\"\u003emethod\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eRequired.\u003c/strong\u003e The HTTP method required to invoke this operation. The value MUST be one of the following values: \u003ccode\u003e\"GET\"\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e\"HEAD\"\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e\"POST\"\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e\"PUT\"\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e\"PATCH\"\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e\"DELETE\"\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e\"OPTIONS\"\u003c/code\u003e. The values MUST be in uppercase.\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-operationsummary\"\u003esummary\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eA short summary of what the operation does. For maximum readability in the swagger-ui, this field SHOULD be less than 120 characters.\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-operationnotes\"\u003enotes\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eA verbose explanation of the operation behavior.\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-operationnickname\"\u003enickname\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eRequired.\u003c/strong\u003e A unique id for the operation that can be used by tools reading the output for further and easier manipulation. For example, Swagger-Codegen will use the nickname as the method name of the operation in the client it generates. The value MUST be alphanumeric and may include underscores. Whitespace characters are not allowed.\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-operationauthorizations\"\u003eauthorizations\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e\u003ca href=\"#5210-authorizations-object\"\u003eAuthorizations Object\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eA list of authorizations required to execute this operation. While not mandatory, if used, it overrides the value given at the API Declaration's \u003ca href=\"#adAuthorizations\"\u003eauthorizations\u003c/a\u003e. In order to completely remove API Declaration's authorizations completely, an empty object (\u003ccode\u003e{}\u003c/code\u003e) may be applied.\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-operationparameters\"\u003eparameters\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e[\u003ca href=\"#524-parameter-object\"\u003eParameter Object\u003c/a\u003e]\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eRequired.\u003c/strong\u003e The inputs to the operation. If no parameters are needed, an empty array MUST be included.\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-operationresponsemessages\"\u003eresponseMessages\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e[\u003ca href=\"#525-response-message-object\"\u003eResponse Message Object\u003c/a\u003e]\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eLists the possible response statuses that can return from the operation.\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-operationproduces\"\u003eproduces\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e[\u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e]\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eA list of MIME types this operation can produce. This is overrides the global \u003ca href=\"#adProduces\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eproduces\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e definition at the root of the API Declaration. Each \u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e value SHOULD represent a MIME type.\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-operationconsumes\"\u003econsumes\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e[\u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e]\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eA list of MIME types this operation can consume. This is overrides the global \u003ca href=\"#adConsumes\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003econsumes\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e definition at the root of the API Declaration. Each \u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e value SHOULD represent a MIME type.\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-operationdeprecated\"\u003edeprecated\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eDeclares this operation to be deprecated. Usage of the declared operation should be refrained. Valid value MUST be either \u003ccode\u003e\"true\"\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003e\"false\"\u003c/code\u003e. \u003cem\u003eNote:\u003c/em\u003e This field will change to type \u003ccode\u003eboolean\u003c/code\u003e in the future.\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003c/tbody\u003e\n\u003c/table\u003e\u003c/markdown-accessiblity-table\u003e\n\u003cdiv 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe Parameter Object describes a single parameter to be sent in an operation and maps to the \u003ca href=\"#operationParameters\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eparameters\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e field in the \u003ca href=\"#523-operation-object\"\u003eOperation of the other objects in the spec. It follows a subset of the \u003ca href=\"http://json-schema.org/\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eJSON-Schema\u003c/a\u003e specification.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003ePlease note that the Models Object is an object containing other object definitions and as such is structured as follows:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"{\n   \u0026quot;Model1\u0026quot; : {...},\n   \u0026quot;Model2\u0026quot; : {...},\n   ...,\n   \u0026quot;ModelN\u0026quot; : {...}\n}\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e{\u003c/span\u003e\n   \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"Model1\"\u003c/span\u003e : \u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e{\u003c/span\u003e...\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e}\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e,\u003c/span\u003e\n   \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"Model2\"\u003c/span\u003e : \u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e{\u003c/span\u003e...\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e}\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e,\u003c/span\u003e\n   ...\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e,\u003c/span\u003e\n   \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"ModelN\"\u003c/span\u003e : \u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e{\u003c/span\u003e...\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e}\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e}\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cmarkdown-accessiblity-table\u003e\u003ctable\u003e\n\u003cthead\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003cth\u003eField Name\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003cth align=\"center\"\u003eType\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003cth\u003eDescription\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003c/thead\u003e\n\u003ctbody\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-modelsmodelname\"\u003e{Model Name}\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e\u003ca href=\"#527-model-object\"\u003eModel Object\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eA new model definition. Note the actual name of the field is the name you're giving your model. For example, \"Category\", \"Pet\", \"User\".\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003c/tbody\u003e\n\u003c/table\u003e\u003c/markdown-accessiblity-table\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e5.2.7 Model Object\u003c/h4\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-527-model-object\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: 5.2.7 Model Object\" href=\"#527-model-object\"\u003e\u003csvg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eA Model Object holds the definition of a new model for this API Declaration.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eModels in Swagger allow for inheritance. The inheritance is controlled by two fields - \u003ca href=\"#modelSubTypes\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003esubTypes\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e to give the name of the models extending this definition, and \u003ca href=\"#modelDiscriminator\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003ediscriminator\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e to support polymorphism.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cmarkdown-accessiblity-table\u003e\u003ctable\u003e\n\u003cthead\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003cth\u003eField Name\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003cth align=\"center\"\u003eType\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003cth\u003eDescription\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003c/thead\u003e\n\u003ctbody\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-modelid\"\u003eid\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eRequired.\u003c/strong\u003e A unique identifier for the model. This MUST be the name given to \u003ca href=\"#modelsModelname\"\u003e{Model Name}\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-modeldescription\"\u003edescription\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eA brief description of this model.\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-modelrequired\"\u003erequired\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e[\u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e]\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eA definition of which properties MUST exist when a model instance is produced. The values MUST be the \u003ca href=\"#propertiesPropertyName\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003e{Property Name}\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e of one of the \u003ca href=\"#528-properties-object\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eproperties\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-modelproperties\"\u003eproperties\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e\u003ca href=\"#528-properties-object\"\u003eProperties Object\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eRequired.\u003c/strong\u003e A list of properties (fields) that are part of the model\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-modelsubtypes\"\u003esubTypes\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e[\u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e]\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eList of the \u003ca href=\"#modelId\"\u003emodel \u003ccode\u003eid\u003c/code\u003es\u003c/a\u003e that inherit from this model. Sub models inherit all the properties of the parent model. Since inheritance is transitive, if the parent of a model inherits from another model, its sub-model will include all properties. As such, if you have \u003ccode\u003eFoo-\u0026gt;Bar-\u0026gt;Baz\u003c/code\u003e, then Baz will inherit the properties of Bar and Foo. There MUST NOT be a cyclic definition of inheritance. For example, if \u003ccode\u003eFoo -\u0026gt; ... -\u0026gt; Bar\u003c/code\u003e, having \u003ccode\u003eBar -\u0026gt; ... -\u0026gt; Foo\u003c/code\u003e is not allowed. There also MUST NOT be a case of multiple inheritance. For example, \u003ccode\u003eFoo -\u0026gt; Baz \u0026lt;- Bar\u003c/code\u003e is not allowed. A sub-model definition MUST NOT override the \u003ca href=\"#modelProperties\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eproperties\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e of any of its ancestors. All sub-models MUST be defined in the same \u003ca href=\"#52-api-declaration\"\u003eAPI Declaration\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ca name=\"user-content-modeldiscriminator\"\u003ediscriminator\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eMUST be included only if \u003ca href=\"#modelSubTypes\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003esubTypes\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e is included. This field allows for polymorphism within the described inherited models. This field MAY be included at any base model but MUST NOT be included in a sub-model. The value of this field MUST be a name of one of the \u003ca href=\"#modelProperties\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eproperties\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e in this model, and that field MUST be in the \u003ca href=\"#modelRequired\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003erequired\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e list. When used, the value of the \u003cem\u003ediscriminator property\u003c/em\u003e MUST be the name of the parent model or any of its sub-models (to any depth of inheritance).\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003c/tbody\u003e\n\u003c/table\u003e\u003c/markdown-accessiblity-table\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch5 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e5.2.7.1 Object Example\u003c/h5\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-5271-object-example\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: 5.2.7.1 Object 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"{\n  \u0026quot;id\u0026quot;: \u0026quot;Order\u0026quot;,\n  \u0026quot;properties\u0026quot;: {\n    \u0026quot;id\u0026quot;: {\n API. If used in the API Declaration's \u003ca href=\"#adAuthorizations\"\u003eauthorizations\u003c/a\u003e, it applies to all operations listed. If used in the Operation's \u003ca href=\"#operationAuthorizations\"\u003eauthorizations\u003c/a\u003e, it applies to the operation itself and may override the API Declaration's authorizations.\nIf multiple authorization schemes are described, they are \u003cstrong\u003eall\u003c/strong\u003e required to perform the operations listed.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003ePlease note that the Authorizations Object is an object containing arrays of object definitions and as such is structured as follows:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"{\n   \u0026quot;Authorization1\u0026quot; The name given to the {Authorization Name} MUST be a friendly name that was given to an authorization scheme in the Resource Listing's \u003ca href=\"#rlAuthorizations\"\u003eauthorizations\u003c/a\u003e.
