</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">4.3.2 <code>void</code></h4><a id="user-content-432-void" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 4.3.2 void" href="#432-void"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This value type is used to indicate that an <a href="#523-operation-object">operation</a> returns no value. As such it MAY be used only for the return type of operations.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">4.3.3 Data Type Fields</h4><a id="user-content-433-data-type-fields" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 4.3.3 Data Type Fields" href="#433-data-type-fields"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">As explained above, when an object is said to include a data type, there are a set of fields it may include (some are required and some are optional).</p>
<p dir="auto">Special care should be taken when referencing a model (or a complex type). There currently two variations, and the proper variation should be documented everywhere it may be used. This behavior will be unified in future versions of the spec.</p>
<p dir="auto">The table below shows the available fields to describe a data type. The <code>Validity</code> column may impose additional restrictions as to which data type is required in order to include this field. For example, <a href="#dataTypeEnum"><code>enum</code></a> may only be included if the <a href="#dataTypeType"><code>type</code></a> field is set to <code>string</code>.</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field Name</th>
<th align="center">Type</th>
<th>Validity</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-datatypetype">type</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td>Any</td>
<td><strong>Required (if <a href="#dataTypeRef"><code>$ref</code></a> is not used).</strong> The return type of the operation. The value MUST be one of the <a href="#431-primitives">Primitives</a>, <code>array</code> or a model's <a href="#modelId"><code>id</code></a>.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-datatyperef">$ref</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td>Any</td>
<td><strong>Required (if <a href="#dataTypeType"><code>type</code></a> is not used).</strong> The <a href="#527-model-object">Model</a> to be used. The value MUST be a model's <a href="#modelId"><code>id</code></a>.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-datatypeformat">format</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td>primitive</td>
<td>Fine-tuned primitive type definition. See <a href="#431-primitives">Primitives</a> for further information. The value MUST be one that is defined under <a href="#431-primitives">Primitives</a>, corresponding to the right primitive <a href="#dataTypeType"><code>type</code></a>.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-datatypedefaultvalue">defaultValue</a></td>
<td align="center"><em>special</em></td>
<td>primitive</td>
<td>The default value to be used for the field. The value type MUST conform with the primitive's <a href="#dataTypeType"><code>type</code></a> value.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-datatypeenum">enum</a></td>
<td align="center">[<code>string</code>]</td>
<td><code>string</code></td>
<td>A fixed list of possible values. If this field is used in conjunction with the <a href="#dataTypeDefaultValue"><code>defaultValue</code></a> field, then the default value MUST be one of the values defined in the <code>enum</code>.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-datatypeminimum">minimum</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td><code>number</code>, <code>integer</code></td>
<td>The minimum valid value for the type, inclusive. If this field is used in conjunction with the <a href="#dataTypeDefaultValue"><code>defaultValue</code></a> field, then the default value MUST be higher than or equal to this value. The value type is <code>string</code> and should represent the minimum numeric value. <strong>Note</strong>: This will change to a numeric value in the future.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-datatypemaximum">maximum</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td><code>number</code>, <code>integer</code></td>
<td>The maximum valid value for the type, inclusive. If this field is used in conjunction with the <a href="#dataTypeDefaultValue"><code>defaultValue</code></a> field, then the default value MUST be lower than or equal to this value. The value type is <code>string</code> and should represent the maximum numeric value. <strong>Note</strong>: This will change to a numeric value in the future.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-datatypeitems">items</a></td>
<td align="center"><a href="#434-items-object">Items Object</a></td>
<td><code>array</code></td>
<td><strong>Required.</strong> The type definition of the values in the container. A container MUST NOT be nested in another container.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-datatypeuniqueitems">uniqueItems</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>boolean</code></td>
<td><code>array</code></td>
<td>A flag to note whether the container allows duplicate values or not. If the value is set to <code>true</code>, then the <code>array</code> acts as a set.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">4.3.4 Items Object</h4><a id="user-content-434-items-object" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 4.3.4 Items Object" href="#434-items-object"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This object is used to describe the value types used inside an array. Of the <a href="#433-data-type-fields">Data Type Fields</a>, it can include either the <a href="#dataTypeType"><code>type</code></a> and <a href="#dataTypeFormat"><code>format</code></a> fields <em>OR</em> the <a href="#dataTypeRef"><code>$ref</code></a> field (when referencing a model). The rest of the listed Data Type fields are not applicable.</p>
<p dir="auto">If the <a href="#dataTypeType"><code>type</code></a> field is included it MUST NOT have the value <code>array</code>. There's currently no support for containers within containers.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h5 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">4.3.4.1 Object Examples</h5><a id="user-content-4341-object-examples" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 4.3.4.1 Object Examples" href="#4341-object-examples"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For a primitive type:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;type&quot;: &quot;string&quot;
}"><pre><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"string"</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">For a complex type (model):</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;$ref&quot;: &quot;Pet&quot;
}"><pre><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"$ref"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Pet"</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">4.3.5 <code>File</code></h4><a id="user-content-435-file" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 4.3.5 File" href="#435-file"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The <code>File</code> (case sensitive) is a special type used to denote file upload. Note that declaring a model with the name <code>File</code> may lead to various conflicts with third party tools and SHOULD be avoided.</p>
<p dir="auto">When using <code>File</code>, the <a href="#operationConsumes"><code>consumes</code></a> field MUST be <code>"multipart/form-data"</code>, and the <a href="#parameterParamType"><code>paramType</code></a> MUST be <code>"form"</code>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5. Schema</h2><a id="user-content-5-schema" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5. Schema" href="#5-schema"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.1 Resource Listing</h3><a id="user-content-51-resource-listing" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.1 Resource Listing" href="#51-resource-listing"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The Resource Listing serves as the root document for the API description. It contains general information about the API and an inventory of the available resources.</p>
<p dir="auto">By default, this document SHOULD be served at the <code>/api-docs</code> path.</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field Name</th>
<th align="center">Type</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-rlswaggerversion">swaggerVersion</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td><strong>Required.</strong> Specifies the Swagger Specification version being used. It can be used by the Swagger UI and other clients to interpret the API listing. The value MUST be an existing Swagger specification version. <br>Currently, <code>"1.0"</code>, <code>"1.1"</code>, <code>"1.2"</code> are valid values. The field is a <code>string</code> type for possible non-numeric versions in the future (for example, "1.2a").</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-rlapis">apis</a></td>
<td align="center">[ <a href="#512-resource-object">Resource Object</a> ]</td>
<td><strong>Required.</strong> Lists the resources to be described by this specification implementation. The array can have 0 or more elements.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-rlapiversion">apiVersion</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td>Provides the version of the application API (not to be confused by the <a href="#rlSwaggerVersion">specification version</a>).</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-rlinfo">info</a></td>
<td align="center"><a href="#513-info-object">Info Object</a></td>
<td>Provides metadata about the API. The metadata can be used by the clients if needed, and can be presented in the Swagger-UI for convenience.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-rlauthorizations">authorizations</a></td>
<td align="center"><a href="#514-authorizations-object">Authorizations Object</a></td>
<td>Provides information about the authorization schemes allowed on this API.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.1.2 Resource Object</h4><a id="user-content-512-resource-object" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.1.2 Resource Object" href="#512-resource-object"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The Resource object describes a <a href="#definitionResource">resource</a> API endpoint in the application.</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field Name</th>
<th align="center">Type</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-aepath">path</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td><strong>Required.</strong> A relative path to the <a href="#52-api-declaration">API declaration</a> from the path used to retrieve this Resource Listing. This <code>path</code> does not necessarily have to correspond to the URL which actually serves this resource in the API but rather where the resource listing itself is served. The value SHOULD be in a relative (URL) path format.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-aedescription">description</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td><em>Recommended.</em> A short description of the resource.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h5 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.1.2.1 Object Example:</h5><a id="user-content-5121-object-example" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.1.2.1 Object Example:" href="#5121-object-example"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
    &quot;path&quot;: &quot;/pets&quot;,
    &quot;description&quot;: &quot;Operations about pets.&quot;
}"><pre><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"path"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"/pets"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"description"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Operations about pets."</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.1.3 Info Object</h4><a id="user-content-513-info-object" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.1.3 Info Object" href="#513-info-object"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The object provides metadata about the API. The metadata can be used by the clients if needed, and can be presented in the Swagger-UI for convenience.</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field Name</th>
<th align="center">Type</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-infotitle">title</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td><strong>Required.</strong> The title of the application.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-infodescription">description</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td><strong>Required.</strong> A short description of the application.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-infotermsofserviceurl">termsOfServiceUrl</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td>A URL to the Terms of Service of the API.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-infocontact">contact</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td>An email to be used for API-related correspondence.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-infolicense">license</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td>The license name used for the API.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-infolicenseurl">licenseUrl</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td>A URL to the license used for the API.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h5 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.1.3.1 Object Example:</h5><a id="user-content-5131-object-example" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.1.3.1 Object Example:" href="#5131-object-example"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.1.4 Authorizations Object</h4><a id="user-content-514-authorizations-object" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.1.4 Authorizations Object" href="#514-authorizations-object"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The object provides information about the authorization schemes provided on this API.
Currently, Swagger supports three authorization schemes - basic authentication, API key and OAuth2.
The Authorizations Object is used only to <em>declare</em> the available authorization schemes but not say which are required where.
The actual authorization restrictions are done at the <a href="#52-api-declaration">API declaration</a> level.</p>
<p dir="auto">Please note that the Authorizations Object is an object containing other object definitions and as such is structured as follows:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
   &quot;Authorization1&quot; : {...},
   &quot;Authorization2&quot; : {...},
   ...,
   &quot;AuthorizationN&quot; : {...}
}"><pre><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
   <span class="pl-s">"Authorization1"</span> : <span class="pl-kos">{</span>...<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
   <span class="pl-s">"Authorization2"</span> : <span class="pl-kos">{</span>...<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
   ...<span class="pl-kos">,</span>
   <span class="pl-s">"AuthorizationN"</span> : <span class="pl-kos">{</span>...<span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field Name</th>
<th align="center">Type</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-authorizationsauthorizationname">{Authorization Name}</a></td>
<td align="center"><a href="#515-authorization-object">Authorization Object</a></td>
<td>A new authorization definition. The name given to the {Authorization Name} is a friendly name that should be used when referring to the authorization scheme. In many cases, the {Authorization Name} used is the same as its type, but it can be anything.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h5 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.1.4.1 Object Example:</h5><a id="user-content-5141-object-example" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.1.4.1 Object Example:" href="#5141-object-example"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.1.5 Authorization Object</h4><a id="user-content-515-authorization-object" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.1.5 Authorization Object" href="#515-authorization-object"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The object provides information about a specific authorization scheme. Currently, the authorization schemes supported are basic authentication, API key and OAuth2.</p>
<p dir="auto">Within OAuth2, the Authorization Code Grant and Implicit Grant are supported.</p>
<p dir="auto">In the table below, the <code>Validity</code> column imposes additional limitations to the requirement of the <a href="#authorizationType"><code>type</code></a> in order to be able to use that field.</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field Name</th>
<th align="center">Type</th>
<th>Validity</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-authorizationtype">type</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td>Any</td>
<td><strong>Required.</strong> The type of the authorization scheme. Values MUST be either <code>"basicAuth"</code>, <code>"apiKey"</code> or <code>"oauth2"</code>.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-authorizationpassas">passAs</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td><code>apiKey</code></td>
<td><strong>Required.</strong> Denotes how the API key must be passed. Valid values are <code>"header"</code> or <code>"query"</code>.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-authorizationkeyname">keyname</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td><code>apiKey</code></td>
<td><strong>Required.</strong> The name of the <code>header</code> or <code>query</code> parameter to be used when passing the API key.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-authorizationscopes">scopes</a></td>
<td align="center">[<a href="#516-scope-object">Scope Object</a>]</td>
<td><code>oauth2</code></td>
<td>A list of supported OAuth2 scopes.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-authorizationgranttypes">grantTypes</a></td>
<td align="center"><a href="#517-grant-types-object">Grant Types Object</a></td>
<td><code>oauth2</code></td>
<td><strong>Required.</strong> Detailed information about the grant types supported by the OAuth2 authorization scheme.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h5 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.1.5.1 Object Example:</h5><a id="user-content-5151-object-example" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.1.5.1 Object Example:" href="#5151-object-example"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.1.6 Scope Object</h4><a id="user-content-516-scope-object" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.1.6 Scope Object" href="#516-scope-object"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Describes an OAuth2 authorization scope.</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field Name</th>
<th align="center">Type</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-scopescope">scope</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td><strong>Required.</strong> The name of the scope.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-scope">description</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td><em>Recommended.</em> A short description of the scope.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.1.7 Grant Types Object</h4><a id="user-content-517-grant-types-object" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.1.7 Grant Types Object" href="#517-grant-types-object"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Provides details regarding the OAuth2 grant types that are supported by the API. Currently, the Authorization Code and Implicit grants are supported.</p>
<p dir="auto">At least one of the grant types MUST be included (otherwise there's no need for the OAuth2 declaration).</p>

</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-granttypesimplicit">implicit</a></td>
<td align="center"><a href="#518-implicit-object">Implicit Object</a></td>
<td>The Implicit Grant flow definition.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-granttypesauthorizationcode">authorization_code</a></td>
<td align="center"><a href="#519-authorization-code-object">Authorization Code Object</a></td>
<td>The Authorization Code Grant flow definition.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>

</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h5 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.1.11.1 Object Example:</h5><a id="user-content-51111-object-example" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.1.11.1 Object Example:" href="#51111-object-example"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;url&quot;: &quot;http://petstore.swagger.wordnik.com/oauth/requestToken&quot;,
  &quot;clientIdName&quot;: &quot;client_id&quot;,
  &quot;clientSecretName&quot;: &quot;client_secret&quot;
}"><pre><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"url"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"http://petstore.swagger.wordnik.com/oauth/requestToken"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"clientIdName"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"client_id"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"clientSecretName"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"client_secret"</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.1.12 Token Endpoint Object</h4><a id="user-content-5112-token-endpoint-object" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.1.12 Token Endpoint Object" href="#5112-token-endpoint-object"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Provides details regarding the OAuth2's <em>Token Endpoint</em>.</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field Name</th>
<th align="center">Type</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-teurl">url</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td><strong>Required.</strong> The URL of the token endpoint for the authentication code grant flow. The value SHOULD be in a URL format.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-tretokenname">tokenName</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td>An optional alternative name to standard "access_token" OAuth2 parameter.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h5 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.1.12.1 Object Example:</h5><a id="user-content-51121-object-example" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.1.12.1 Object Example:" href="#51121-object-example"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;url&quot;: &quot;http://petstore.swagger.wordnik.com/oauth/token&quot;,
  &quot;tokenName&quot;: &quot;access_code&quot;
}"><pre><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"url"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"http://petstore.swagger.wordnik.com/oauth/token"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"tokenName"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"access_code"</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.2 API Declaration</h3><a id="user-content-52-api-declaration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.2 API Declaration" href="#52-api-declaration"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The API Declaration provides information about an API exposed on a resource. There should be one file per <a href="#512-resource-object">Resource</a> described. The file MUST be served in the URL described by the <a href="#aePath"><code>path</code></a> field.</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field Name</th>
<th align="center">Type</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-adswaggerversion">swaggerVersion</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td><strong>Required.</strong> Specifies the Swagger Specification version being used. It can be used by the Swagger UI and other clients to interpret the API listing. The value MUST be an existing Swagger specification version. <br>Currently, <code>"1.0"</code>, <code>"1.1"</code>, <code>"1.2"</code> are valid values.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-adapiversion">apiVersion</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td>Provides the version of the application API (not to be confused by the <a href="#adSwaggerVersion">specification version</a>).</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-adbasepath">basePath</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td><strong>Required.</strong> The root URL serving the API. This field is important because while it is common to have the Resource Listing and API Declarations on the server providing the APIs themselves, it is not a requirement. The API specifications can be served using static files and not generated by the API server itself, so the URL for serving the API cannot always be derived from the URL serving the API specification. The value SHOULD be in the format of a URL.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-adresourcepath">resourcePath</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td>The <em>relative</em> path to the resource, from the <a href="#adBasePath"><code>basePath</code></a>, which this API Specification describes. The value MUST precede with a forward slash (<code>"/"</code>).</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-adapis">apis</a></td>
<td align="center">[<a href="#522-api-object">API Object</a>]</td>
<td><strong>Required.</strong> A list of the APIs exposed on this resource. There MUST NOT be more than one API Object per <a href="#apiPath"><code>path</code></a> in the array.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-admodels">models</a></td>
<td align="center"><a href="#526-models-object">Models Object</a></td>
<td>A list of the models available to this resource. Note that these need to be exposed separately for each API Declaration.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-adproduces">produces</a></td>
<td align="center">[<code>string</code>]</td>
<td>A list of MIME types the APIs on this resource can produce. This is global to all APIs but can be overridden on specific API calls.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-adconsumes">consumes</a></td>
<td align="center">[<code>string</code>]</td>
<td>A list of MIME types the APIs on this resource can consume. This is global to all APIs but can be overridden on specific API calls.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-adauthorizations">authorizations</a></td>
<td align="center"><a href="#5210-authorizations-object">Authorizations Object</a></td>
<td>A list of authorizations schemes <em>required</em> for the operations listed in this API declaration. Individual operations may override this setting. If there are multiple authorization schemes described here, it means they're <strong>all</strong> applied.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.2.1 Object Example</h4><a id="user-content-521-object-example" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.2.1 Object Example" href="#521-object-example"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

            <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
              <span class="pl-s">"code"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">400</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
              <span class="pl-s">"message"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Invalid ID supplied"</span>
            <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
            <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
              <span class="pl-s">"code"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">404</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
              <span class="pl-s">"message"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Order not found"</span>
            <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
          <span class="pl-kos">]</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">]</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-s">"path"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"/store/order"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-s">"operations"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
          <span class="pl-s">"method"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"POST"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
          <span class="pl-s">"summary"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Place an order for a pet"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
          <span class="pl-s">"notes"</span>: <span class="pl-s">""</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
          <span class="pl-s">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"void"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
          <span class="pl-s">"nickname"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"placeOrder"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
          <span class="pl-s">"authorizations"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
            <span class="pl-s">"oauth2"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
              <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
                <span class="pl-s">"scope"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"test:anything"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
                <span class="pl-s">"description"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"anything"</span>
              <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
            <span class="pl-kos">]</span>
          <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
          <span class="pl-s">"parameters"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
            <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
              <span class="pl-s">"name"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"body"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
              <span class="pl-s">"description"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"order placed for purchasing the pet"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
              <span class="pl-s">"required"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
              <span class="pl-s">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Order"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
              <span class="pl-s">"paramType"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"body"</span>
            <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
          <span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
          <span class="pl-s">"responseMessages"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
            <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
              <span class="pl-s">"code"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">400</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
              <span class="pl-s">"message"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Invalid order"</span>
            <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
          <span class="pl-kos">]</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">]</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"models"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"Order"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-s">"id"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Order"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-s">"properties"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-s">"id"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
          <span class="pl-s">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"integer"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
          <span class="pl-s">"format"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"int64"</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-s">"petId"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
          <span class="pl-s">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"integer"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
          <span class="pl-s">"format"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"int64"</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-s">"quantity"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
          <span class="pl-s">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"integer"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
          <span class="pl-s">"format"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"int32"</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-s">"status"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
          <span class="pl-s">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"string"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
          <span class="pl-s">"description"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Order Status"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
          <span class="pl-s">"enum"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
            <span class="pl-s">"placed"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
            <span class="pl-s">"approved"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
            <span class="pl-s">"delivered"</span>
          <span class="pl-kos">]</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-s">"shipDate"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
          <span class="pl-s">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"string"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
          <span class="pl-s">"format"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"date-time"</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.2.2 API Object</h4><a id="user-content-522-api-object" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.2.2 API Object" href="#522-api-object"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The API Object describes one or more operations on a single <a href="#apiPath"><code>path</code></a>. In the <a href="#adApis"><code>apis</code></a> array, there MUST be only one <a href="#522-api-object"><code>API Object</code></a> per <a href="#apiPath"><code>path</code></a>.</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field Name</th>
<th align="center">Type</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-apipath">path</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td><strong>Required.</strong> The relative path to the operation, from the <a href="#adBasePath"><code>basePath</code></a>, which this operation describes. The value SHOULD be in a relative (URL) path format.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/OAI/OpenAPI-Specification/blob/main/versions/apiDescription">description</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td><em>Recommended.</em> A short description of the resource.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/OAI/OpenAPI-Specification/blob/main/versions/apiOperations">operations</a></td>
<td align="center">[<a href="#523-operation-object">Operation Object</a>]</td>
<td><strong>Required.</strong> A list of the API operations available on this path. The array may include 0 or more operations. There MUST NOT be more than one Operation Object per <a href="#operationMethod"><code>method</code></a> in the array.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h5 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.2.2.1 Object Example:</h5><a id="user-content-5221-object-example" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.2.2.1 Object Example:" href="#5221-object-example"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.2.3 Operation Object</h4><a id="user-content-523-operation-object" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.2.3 Operation Object" href="#523-operation-object"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The Operation Object describes a single operation on a <a href="#apiPath"><code>path</code></a>.</p>
<p dir="auto">In the <a href="#apiOperations"><code>operations</code></a> array, there MUST be only one <a href="#523-operation-object"><code>Operation Object</code></a> per <a href="#operationMethod"><code>method</code></a>.</p>
<p dir="auto">This object includes the <a href="#433-data-type-fields">Data Type Fields</a> in order to describe the return value of the operation. The <a href="#dataTypeType"><code>type</code></a> field MUST be used to link to other models.</p>
<p dir="auto">This is the only object where the <a href="#dataTypeType"><code>type</code></a> MAY have the value of <a href="#432-void"><code>void</code></a> to indicate that the operation returns no value.</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field Name</th>
<th align="center">Type</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-operationmethod">method</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td><strong>Required.</strong> The HTTP method required to invoke this operation. The value MUST be one of the following values: <code>"GET"</code>, <code>"HEAD"</code>, <code>"POST"</code>, <code>"PUT"</code>, <code>"PATCH"</code>, <code>"DELETE"</code>, <code>"OPTIONS"</code>. The values MUST be in uppercase.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-operationsummary">summary</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td>A short summary of what the operation does. For maximum readability in the swagger-ui, this field SHOULD be less than 120 characters.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-operationnotes">notes</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td>A verbose explanation of the operation behavior.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-operationnickname">nickname</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td><strong>Required.</strong> A unique id for the operation that can be used by tools reading the output for further and easier manipulation. For example, Swagger-Codegen will use the nickname as the method name of the operation in the client it generates. The value MUST be alphanumeric and may include underscores. Whitespace characters are not allowed.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-operationauthorizations">authorizations</a></td>
<td align="center"><a href="#5210-authorizations-object">Authorizations Object</a></td>
<td>A list of authorizations required to execute this operation. While not mandatory, if used, it overrides the value given at the API Declaration's <a href="#adAuthorizations">authorizations</a>. In order to completely remove API Declaration's authorizations completely, an empty object (<code>{}</code>) may be applied.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-operationparameters">parameters</a></td>
<td align="center">[<a href="#524-parameter-object">Parameter Object</a>]</td>
<td><strong>Required.</strong> The inputs to the operation. If no parameters are needed, an empty array MUST be included.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-operationresponsemessages">responseMessages</a></td>
<td align="center">[<a href="#525-response-message-object">Response Message Object</a>]</td>
<td>Lists the possible response statuses that can return from the operation.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-operationproduces">produces</a></td>
<td align="center">[<code>string</code>]</td>
<td>A list of MIME types this operation can produce. This is overrides the global <a href="#adProduces"><code>produces</code></a> definition at the root of the API Declaration. Each <code>string</code> value SHOULD represent a MIME type.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-operationconsumes">consumes</a></td>
<td align="center">[<code>string</code>]</td>
<td>A list of MIME types this operation can consume. This is overrides the global <a href="#adConsumes"><code>consumes</code></a> definition at the root of the API Declaration. Each <code>string</code> value SHOULD represent a MIME type.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-operationdeprecated">deprecated</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td>Declares this operation to be deprecated. Usage of the declared operation should be refrained. Valid value MUST be either <code>"true"</code> or <code>"false"</code>. <em>Note:</em> This field will change to type <code>boolean</code> in the future.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h5 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.2.3.1 Object Example</h5><a id="user-content-5231-object-example" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.2.3.1 Object Example" href="#5231-object-example"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="        {
          &quot;method&quot;: &quot;GET&quot;,
          &quot;summary&quot;: &quot;Find pet by ID&quot;,
          &quot;notes&quot;: &quot;Returns a pet based on ID&quot;,
          &quot;type&quot;: &quot;Pet&quot;,

            {

          <span class="pl-s">"method"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"GET"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>

            <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
              <span class="pl-s">"name"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"petId"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
              <span class="pl-s">"description"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"ID of pet that needs to be fetched"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
              <span class="pl-s">"required"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
              <span class="pl-s">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"integer"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
              <span class="pl-s">"format"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"int64"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
              <span class="pl-s">"paramType"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"path"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
              <span class="pl-s">"minimum"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"1.0"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
              <span class="pl-s">"maximum"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"100000.0"</span>
            <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
          <span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>

            <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
