<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.2.4 Parameter Object</h4><a id="user-content-524-parameter-object" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.2.4 Parameter Object" href="#524-parameter-object"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The Parameter Object describes a single parameter to be sent in an operation and maps to the <a href="#operationParameters"><code>parameters</code></a> field in the <a href="#523-operation-object">Operation Object</a>.</p>
<p dir="auto">This object includes the <a href="#433-data-type-fields">Data Type Fields</a> in order to describe the type of this parameter. The <a href="#dataTypeType"><code>type</code></a> field MUST be used to link to other models.</p>
<p dir="auto">If <a href="#dataTypeType"><code>type</code></a> is <a href="#434-file"><code>File</code></a>, the <a href="#operationConsumes"><code>consumes</code></a> field MUST be <code>"multipart/form-data"</code>, and the <a href="#parameterParamType"><code>paramType</code></a> MUST be <code>"form"</code>.</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field Name</th>
<th align="center">Type</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-parameterparamtype">paramType</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td><strong>Required.</strong> The type of the parameter (that is, the location of the parameter in the request). The value MUST be one of these values: <code>"path"</code>, <code>"query"</code>, <code>"body"</code>, <code>"header"</code>, <code>"form"</code>. Note that the values MUST be lower case.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-parametername">name</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td><strong>Required.</strong> The unique name for the parameter. Each <code>name</code> MUST be unique, even if they are associated with different <code>paramType</code> values. Parameter names are <em>case sensitive</em>. <ul dir="auto"><li>If <a href="#parameterParamType"><code>paramType</code></a> is <code>"path"</code>, the <code>name</code> field MUST correspond to the associated path segment from the <a href="#apiPath"><code>path</code></a> field in the <a href="#522-api-object">API Object</a>. </li><li>If <a href="#parameterParamType"><code>paramType</code></a> is <code>"query"</code>, the <code>name</code> field corresponds to the query parameter name. </li><li>If <a href="#parameterParamType"><code>paramType</code></a> is <code>"body"</code>, the name is used only for Swagger-UI and Swagger-Codegen. In this case, the <code>name</code> MUST be <code>"body"</code>. </li><li>If <a href="#parameterParamType"><code>paramType</code></a> is <code>"form"</code>, the <code>name</code> field corresponds to the form parameter key. </li><li>If <a href="#parameterParamType"><code>paramType</code></a> is <code>"header"</code>, the <code>name</code> field corresponds to the header parameter key. </li></ul> See <a href="#5241-name-examples">here</a> for some examples.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-parameterdescription">description</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td><em>Recommended.</em> A brief description of this parameter.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-parameterrequired">required</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>boolean</code></td>
<td>A flag to note whether this parameter is required. If this field is not included, it is equivalent to adding this field with the value <code>false</code>. If <a href="#parameterParamType"><code>paramType</code></a> is <code>"path"</code> then this field MUST be included and have the value <code>true</code>.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-parameterallowmultiple">allowMultiple</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>boolean</code></td>
<td>Another way to allow multiple values for a "query" parameter. If used, the query parameter may accept comma-separated values. The field may be used only if <a href="#parameterParamType"><code>paramType</code></a> is <code>"query"</code>, <code>"header"</code> or <code>"path"</code>.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h5 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.2.4.1 Name Examples</h5><a id="user-content-5241-name-examples" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.2.4.1 Name Examples" href="#5241-name-examples"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">If <a href="#parameterParamType"><code>paramType</code></a> is <code>"path"</code>, and assuming the <code>path</code> is <code>"/pet/{id}"</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=""><pre></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">"name": "id"
```</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">If <a href="#parameterParamType"><code>paramType</code></a> is <code>"query"</code>, and assuming the URL call is <code>"http://host/resource?limit=100"</code> (that is, there's a query parameter called <code>"limit"</code>):</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=""><pre></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">"name": "limit"
```</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">If <a href="#parameterParamType"><code>paramType</code></a> is <code>"body"</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=""><pre></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">"name": "body"
```</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h5 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.2.4.2 Object Example</h5><a id="user-content-5242-object-example" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.2.4.2 Object Example" href="#5242-object-example"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;name&quot;: &quot;body&quot;,
  &quot;description&quot;: &quot;Pet object that needs to be updated in the store&quot;,
  &quot;required&quot;: true,
  &quot;type&quot;: &quot;Pet&quot;,
  &quot;paramType&quot;: &quot;body&quot;
}"><pre><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"name"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"body"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"description"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Pet object that needs to be updated in the store"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"required"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Pet"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"paramType"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"body"</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.2.5 Response Message Object</h4><a id="user-content-525-response-message-object" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.2.5 Response Message Object" href="#525-response-message-object"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The Response Message Object describes a single possible response message that can be returned from the operation call, and maps to the <a href="#operationResponseMessages"><code>responseMessages</code></a> field in the <a href="#523-operation-object">Operation Object</a>. Each Response Message allows you to give further details as to why the HTTP status code may be received.</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field Name</th>
<th align="center">Type</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-rmcode">code</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>integer</code></td>
<td><strong>Required.</strong> The HTTP status code returned. The value SHOULD be one of the status codes as described in <a href="http://www.w3.org/Protocols/rfc2616/rfc2616-sec10.html" rel="nofollow">RFC 2616 - Section 10</a>.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-rmmessage">message</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td><strong>Required.</strong> The explanation for the status code. It SHOULD be the reason an error is received if an error status code is used.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-rmresponsemodel">responseModel</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td>The return type for the given response.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h5 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.2.5.1 Object Example</h5><a id="user-content-5251-object-example" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.2.5.1 Object Example" href="#5251-object-example"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="  {
    &quot;code&quot;: 404,
    &quot;message&quot;: &quot;no project found&quot;,
    &quot;responseModel&quot;: &quot;ErrorModel&quot;
  }"><pre>  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"code"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">404</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"message"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"no project found"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"responseModel"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"ErrorModel"</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.2.6 Models Object</h4><a id="user-content-526-models-object" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.2.6 Models Object" href="#526-models-object"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The Models Object holds a field per model definition, and this is different than the structure of the other objects in the spec. It follows a subset of the <a href="http://json-schema.org/" rel="nofollow">JSON-Schema</a> specification.</p>
<p dir="auto">Please note that the Models Object is an object containing other object definitions and as such is structured as follows:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
   &quot;Model1&quot; : {...},
   &quot;Model2&quot; : {...},
   ...,
   &quot;ModelN&quot; : {...}
}"><pre><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
   <span class="pl-s">"Model1"</span> : <span class="pl-kos">{</span>...<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
   <span class="pl-s">"Model2"</span> : <span class="pl-kos">{</span>...<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
   ...<span class="pl-kos">,</span>
   <span class="pl-s">"ModelN"</span> : <span class="pl-kos">{</span>...<span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field Name</th>
<th align="center">Type</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-modelsmodelname">{Model Name}</a></td>
<td align="center"><a href="#527-model-object">Model Object</a></td>
<td>A new model definition. Note the actual name of the field is the name you're giving your model. For example, "Category", "Pet", "User".</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h5 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.2.6.1 Object Example</h5><a id="user-content-5261-object-example" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.2.6.1 Object Example" href="#5261-object-example"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
    &quot;Category&quot;: {
      &quot;id&quot;: &quot;Category&quot;,
      &quot;properties&quot;: {
        &quot;id&quot;: {
          &quot;type&quot;: &quot;integer&quot;,
          &quot;format&quot;: &quot;int64&quot;
        },
        &quot;name&quot;: {
          &quot;type&quot;: &quot;string&quot;
        }
      }
    }
}"><pre><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"Category"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-s">"id"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Category"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-s">"properties"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-s">"id"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
          <span class="pl-s">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"integer"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
          <span class="pl-s">"format"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"int64"</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-s">"name"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
          <span class="pl-s">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"string"</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.2.7 Model Object</h4><a id="user-content-527-model-object" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.2.7 Model Object" href="#527-model-object"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">A Model Object holds the definition of a new model for this API Declaration.</p>
<p dir="auto">Models in Swagger allow for inheritance. The inheritance is controlled by two fields - <a href="#modelSubTypes"><code>subTypes</code></a> to give the name of the models extending this definition, and <a href="#modelDiscriminator"><code>discriminator</code></a> to support polymorphism.</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field Name</th>
<th align="center">Type</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-modelid">id</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td><strong>Required.</strong> A unique identifier for the model. This MUST be the name given to <a href="#modelsModelname">{Model Name}</a>.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-modeldescription">description</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td>A brief description of this model.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-modelrequired">required</a></td>
<td align="center">[<code>string</code>]</td>
<td>A definition of which properties MUST exist when a model instance is produced. The values MUST be the <a href="#propertiesPropertyName"><code>{Property Name}</code></a> of one of the <a href="#528-properties-object"><code>properties</code></a>.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-modelproperties">properties</a></td>
<td align="center"><a href="#528-properties-object">Properties Object</a></td>
<td><strong>Required.</strong> A list of properties (fields) that are part of the model</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-modelsubtypes">subTypes</a></td>
<td align="center">[<code>string</code>]</td>
<td>List of the <a href="#modelId">model <code>id</code>s</a> that inherit from this model. Sub models inherit all the properties of the parent model. Since inheritance is transitive, if the parent of a model inherits from another model, its sub-model will include all properties. As such, if you have <code>Foo-&gt;Bar-&gt;Baz</code>, then Baz will inherit the properties of Bar and Foo. There MUST NOT be a cyclic definition of inheritance. For example, if <code>Foo -&gt; ... -&gt; Bar</code>, having <code>Bar -&gt; ... -&gt; Foo</code> is not allowed. There also MUST NOT be a case of multiple inheritance. For example, <code>Foo -&gt; Baz &lt;- Bar</code> is not allowed. A sub-model definition MUST NOT override the <a href="#modelProperties"><code>properties</code></a> of any of its ancestors. All sub-models MUST be defined in the same <a href="#52-api-declaration">API Declaration</a>.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-modeldiscriminator">discriminator</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td>MUST be included only if <a href="#modelSubTypes"><code>subTypes</code></a> is included. This field allows for polymorphism within the described inherited models. This field MAY be included at any base model but MUST NOT be included in a sub-model. The value of this field MUST be a name of one of the <a href="#modelProperties"><code>properties</code></a> in this model, and that field MUST be in the <a href="#modelRequired"><code>required</code></a> list. When used, the value of the <em>discriminator property</em> MUST be the name of the parent model or any of its sub-models (to any depth of inheritance).</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h5 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.2.7.1 Object Example</h5><a id="user-content-5271-object-example" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.2.7.1 Object Example" href="#5271-object-example"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h5 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.2.7.2 Inheritance Example</h5><a id="user-content-5272-inheritance-example" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.2.7.2 Inheritance Example" href="#5272-inheritance-example"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Say we have a general Animal model, and a sub-model for Cat.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&quot;Animal&quot;: {
  &quot;id&quot;: &quot;Animal&quot;,

  &quot;properties&quot;: {

  ],
  &quot;properties&quot;: {
    &quot;likesMilk&quot;: {
      &quot;type&quot;: &quot;boolean&quot;
    }
  },
}"><pre><span class="pl-s">"Animal"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

  <span class="pl-s">"required"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"id"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"type"</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"properties"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"id"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>

      <span class="pl-s">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"string"</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.2.8 Properties Object</h4><a id="user-content-528-properties-object" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.2.8 Properties Object" href="#528-properties-object"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The Properties Object holds a field per property definition, and this is different than the structure of the other objects in the spec. It follows a subset of the <a href="http://json-schema.org/" rel="nofollow">JSON-Schema</a> specification.</p>
<p dir="auto">Please note that the Properties Object is an object containing other object definitions and as such is structured as follows:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
   &quot;Property1&quot; : {...},
   &quot;Property2&quot; : {...},
   ...,
   &quot;PropertyN&quot; : {...}
}"><pre><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
   <span class="pl-s">"Property1"</span> : <span class="pl-kos">{</span>...<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
   <span class="pl-s">"Property2"</span> : <span class="pl-kos">{</span>...<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
   ...<span class="pl-kos">,</span>
   <span class="pl-s">"PropertyN"</span> : <span class="pl-kos">{</span>...<span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field Name</th>
<th align="center">Type</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-propertiespropertyname">{Property Name}</a></td>
<td align="center"><a href="#529-property-object">Property Object</a></td>
<td>A new model property definition. Note the actual name of the field is the name you're giving your property. For example, "id", "name", "age".</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h5 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.2.8.1 Object Example</h5><a id="user-content-5281-object-example" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.2.8.1 Object Example" href="#5281-object-example"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="      {

          &quot;type&quot;: &quot;string&quot;

      }"><pre>      <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-s">"id"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
          <span class="pl-s">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"integer"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
          <span class="pl-s">"format"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"int64"</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-s">"name"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
          <span class="pl-s">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"string"</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.2.9 Property Object</h4><a id="user-content-529-property-object" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.2.9 Property Object" href="#529-property-object"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">A Property Object holds the definition of a new property for a model.</p>
<p dir="auto">This object includes the <a href="#433-data-type-fields">Data Type Fields</a> in order to describe the type of this property. The <a href="#dataTypeRef"><code>$ref</code></a> field MUST be used when linking to other models.</p>
<p dir="auto">Properties MUST NOT contain other properties. If there's a need for an internal object hierarchy, additional models MUST be created and linked to a flat structure.</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field Name</th>
<th align="center">Type</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-propertydescription">description</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td><em>Recommended.</em> A brief description of this property.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h5 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.2.9.1 Object Examples</h5><a id="user-content-5291-object-examples" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.2.9.1 Object Examples" href="#5291-object-examples"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">A simple 64bit integer field called "id", with a description and min/max values:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&quot;id&quot;: {
    &quot;type&quot;: &quot;integer&quot;,
    &quot;format&quot;: &quot;int64&quot;,
    &quot;description&quot;: &quot;unique identifier for the pet&quot;,
    &quot;minimum&quot;: &quot;0.0&quot;,
    &quot;maximum&quot;: &quot;100.0&quot;
}"><pre><span class="pl-s">"id"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"integer"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"format"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"int64"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"description"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"unique identifier for the pet"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"minimum"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"0.0"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"maximum"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"100.0"</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">A "category" field of a Category model.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&quot;category&quot;: {
    &quot;$ref&quot;: &quot;Category&quot;
}"><pre><span class="pl-s">"category"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"$ref"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Category"</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">A "tags" field of type array containing Tag models.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&quot;tags&quot;: {
    &quot;type&quot;: &quot;array&quot;,
    &quot;items&quot;: {
        &quot;$ref&quot;: &quot;Tag&quot;
    }
}"><pre><span class="pl-s">"tags"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"array"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"items"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-s">"$ref"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Tag"</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.2.10 Authorizations Object</h4><a id="user-content-5210-authorizations-object" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.2.10 Authorizations Object" href="#5210-authorizations-object"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The Authorizations Object provides information about the authorization schemes enforced on this API. If used in the API Declaration's <a href="#adAuthorizations">authorizations</a>, it applies to all operations listed. If used in the Operation's <a href="#operationAuthorizations">authorizations</a>, it applies to the operation itself and may override the API Declaration's authorizations.
If multiple authorization schemes are described, they are <strong>all</strong> required to perform the operations listed.</p>
<p dir="auto">Please note that the Authorizations Object is an object containing arrays of object definitions and as such is structured as follows:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
   &quot;Authorization1&quot; : [...],
   &quot;Authorization2&quot; : [...],
   ...,
   &quot;AuthorizationN&quot; : [...]
}"><pre><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
   <span class="pl-s">"Authorization1"</span> : <span class="pl-kos">[</span>...<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
   <span class="pl-s">"Authorization2"</span> : <span class="pl-kos">[</span>...<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
   ...<span class="pl-kos">,</span>
   <span class="pl-s">"AuthorizationN"</span> : <span class="pl-kos">[</span>...<span class="pl-kos">]</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field Name</th>
<th align="center">Type</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-adauthorizationsauthorizationname">{Authorization Name}</a></td>
<td align="center">*</td>
<td>The authorization scheme to be used. The name given to the {Authorization Name} MUST be a friendly name that was given to an authorization scheme in the Resource Listing's <a href="#rlAuthorizations">authorizations</a>. If the friendly name describes an OAuth2 security scheme, the value should be of type [<a href="#5211-scope-object">Scope Object</a>] (but may be an empty array to denote 'no scopes'). For all other authorization scheme types, the value MUST be an empty array.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h5 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.2.10 Object Example:</h5><a id="user-content-5210-object-example" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.2.10 Object Example:" href="#5210-object-example"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;oauth2&quot;: [
    {
      &quot;scope&quot;: &quot;write:pets&quot;,
      &quot;description&quot;: &quot;modify pets in your account&quot;
    },
    {
      &quot;scope&quot;: &quot;read:pets&quot;,
      &quot;description&quot;: &quot;read your pets&quot;
    }
  ]
}"><pre><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"oauth2"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-s">"scope"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"write:pets"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-s">"description"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"modify pets in your account"</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-s">"scope"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"read:pets"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-s">"description"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"read your pets"</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">]</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.2.11 Scope Object</h4><a id="user-content-5211-scope-object" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.2.11 Scope Object" href="#5211-scope-object"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Describes an OAuth2 authorization scope. The scope described here MUST be described in the respective friendly name definition of the security scheme in the Resource Listing's <a href="#rlAuthorizations">authorizations</a>.</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field Name</th>
<th align="center">Type</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-scopescope">scope</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td><strong>Required.</strong> The name of the scope.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a name="user-content-scope">description</a></td>
<td align="center"><code>string</code></td>
<td><em>Recommended.</em> A short description of the scope.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h5 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.2.11.1 Object Example:</h5><a id="user-content-52111-object-example" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.2.11.1 Object Example:" href="#52111-object-example"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
